### [236] [SAEL: Leveraging Large Language Models with Adaptive Mixture-of-Experts for Smart Contract Vulnerability Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22371)
*Lei Yu,Shiqi Cheng,Zhirong Huang,Jingyuan Zhang,Chenjie Shen,Junyi Lu,Li Yang,Fengjun Zhang,Jiajia Ma*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出SAEL框架，一个基于LLM的智能合约漏洞检测方法，通过自适应专家混合架构有效整合LLM预测、解释及代码特征，超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能合约漏洞检测面临挑战：传统静态分析难以应对复杂场景；专用预训练模型泛化能力有限。通用大语言模型（LLMs）虽能适应新漏洞，但在特定类型上表现不如专用模型，但其生成的解释对代码理解有益。因此，研究旨在结合LLMs的优势并利用其解释能力，克服现有方法的局限。

Method: 提出SAEL框架。首先，设计引导性提示词，使LLMs识别漏洞并生成解释作为预测特征。其次，对CodeT5和T5进行提示调优（prompt-tuning），以处理合约代码和解释，提升任务性能。核心是引入自适应专家混合（Adaptive Mixture-of-Experts）架构，通过门控网络（使用TopK过滤、Softmax归一化及多头自注意力机制）动态调整LLM预测、解释特征和代码特征的权重。采用联合损失函数进行梯度优化，以整合并提升整体检测性能。

Result: 实验结果表明，SAEL在多种智能合约漏洞检测方面均优于现有方法。

Conclusion: SAEL是一个创新的智能合约漏洞检测框架，通过有效整合LLM预测、其生成的解释以及代码特征，并采用自适应专家混合架构动态优化特征融合，显著提升了漏洞检测性能，为区块链安全提供了更有效的解决方案。

Abstract: With the increasing security issues in blockchain, smart contract
vulnerability detection has become a research focus. Existing vulnerability
detection methods have their limitations: 1) Static analysis methods struggle
with complex scenarios. 2) Methods based on specialized pre-trained models
perform well on specific datasets but have limited generalization capabilities.
In contrast, general-purpose Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate
impressive ability in adapting to new vulnerability patterns. However, they
often underperform on specific vulnerability types compared to methods based on
specialized pre-trained models. We also observe that explanations generated by
general-purpose LLMs can provide fine-grained code understanding information,
contributing to improved detection performance.
  Inspired by these observations, we propose SAEL, an LLM-based framework for
smart contract vulnerability detection. We first design targeted prompts to
guide LLMs in identifying vulnerabilities and generating explanations, which
serve as prediction features. Next, we apply prompt-tuning on CodeT5 and T5 to
process contract code and explanations, enhancing task-specific performance. To
combine the strengths of each approach, we introduce an Adaptive
Mixture-of-Experts architecture. This dynamically adjusts feature weights via a
Gating Network, which selects relevant features using TopK filtering and
Softmax normalization, and incorporates a Multi-Head Self-Attention mechanism
to enhance cross-feature relationships. This design enables effective
integration of LLM predictions, explanation features, and code features through
gradient optimization. The loss function jointly considers both independent
feature performance and overall weighted predictions. Experiments show that
SAEL outperforms existing methods across various vulnerabilities.

</details>


### [237] [Understanding Concept Drift with Deprecated Permissions in Android Malware Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22231)
*Ahmed Sabbah,Radi Jarrar,Samer Zein,David Mohaisen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 研究调查了废弃和受限的Android权限对机器学习恶意软件检测模型性能的影响，发现其影响甚微，且排除这些权限有助于概念漂移检测和模型优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Android恶意软件检测中，基于权限的机器学习方法忽略了权限保护级别、废弃和受限等因素，这些因素可能导致概念漂移。本研究旨在探讨这些被忽视的因素对模型性能的影响。

Method: 使用包含166个权限和超过70,000个恶意及良性应用的庞大数据集。采用多种机器学习和深度学习算法作为分类器，并结合不同的概念漂移检测策略。此外，还进行了数据集平衡处理。

Result: Android权限是有效的恶意软件检测特征。排除废弃和受限权限对模型性能影响微乎其微，在某些情况下（如CNN）甚至提高了准确性。排除这些权限也增强了逐年分析的概念漂移检测能力。数据集平衡进一步提升了模型性能，减少了低准确率实例，并通过Kolmogorov-Smirnov测试增强了概念漂移检测。

Conclusion: Android权限对于恶意软件检测非常有效。即使排除废弃和受限权限，对模型性能影响甚微，反而有助于提升概念漂移检测能力。数据平衡也对模型性能和漂移检测有积极作用。

Abstract: Permission analysis is a widely used method for Android malware detection. It
involves examining the permissions requested by an application to access
sensitive data or perform potentially malicious actions. In recent years,
various machine learning (ML) algorithms have been applied to Android malware
detection using permission-based features and feature selection techniques,
often achieving high accuracy. However, these studies have largely overlooked
important factors such as protection levels and the deprecation or restriction
of permissions due to updates in the Android OS -- factors that can contribute
to concept drift.
  In this study, we investigate the impact of deprecated and restricted
permissions on the performance of machine learning models. A large dataset
containing 166 permissions was used, encompassing more than 70,000 malware and
benign applications. Various machine learning and deep learning algorithms were
employed as classifiers, along with different concept drift detection
strategies. The results suggest that Android permissions are highly effective
features for malware detection, with the exclusion of deprecated and restricted
permissions having only a marginal impact on model performance. In some cases,
such as with CNN, accuracy improved. Excluding these permissions also enhanced
the detection of concept drift using a year-to-year analysis strategy. Dataset
balancing further improved model performance, reduced low-accuracy instances,
and enhanced concept drift detection via the Kolmogorov-Smirnov test.

</details>


### [238] [Hate in Plain Sight: On the Risks of Moderating AI-Generated Hateful Illusions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22617)
*Yiting Qu,Ziqing Yang,Yihan Ma,Michael Backes,Savvas Zannettou,Yang Zhang*

Result: 1. 现有内容审核模型存在显著漏洞：内容审核分类器的检测准确率低于0.245，视觉语言模型的检测准确率低于0.102。2. 发现这些模型视觉编码器主要关注图像表层细节，未能识别第二层信息（隐藏的仇恨信息）。

Abstract: Recent advances in text-to-image diffusion models have enabled the creation
of a new form of digital art: optical illusions--visual tricks that create
different perceptions of reality. However, adversaries may misuse such
techniques to generate hateful illusions, which embed specific hate messages
into harmless scenes and disseminate them across web communities. In this work,
we take the first step toward investigating the risks of scalable hateful
illusion generation and the potential for bypassing current content moderation
models. Specifically, we generate 1,860 optical illusions using Stable
Diffusion and ControlNet, conditioned on 62 hate messages. Of these, 1,571 are
hateful illusions that successfully embed hate messages, either overtly or
subtly, forming the Hateful Illusion dataset. Using this dataset, we evaluate
the performance of six moderation classifiers and nine vision language models

significant vulnerabilities in existing moderation models: the detection
accuracy falls below 0.245 for moderation classifiers and below 0.102 for VLMs.
We further identify a critical limitation in their vision encoders, which
mainly focus on surface-level image details while overlooking the secondary

preliminary mitigation measures and identify the most effective approaches from

### [239] [Breaking Obfuscation: Cluster-Aware Graph with LLM-Aided Recovery for Malicious JavaScript Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22447)
*Zhihong Liang,Xin Wang,Zhenhuang Hu,Liangliang Song,Lin Chen,Jingjing Guo,Yanbin Wang,Ye Tian*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出DeCoda框架，结合LLM去混淆和代码图学习来检测恶意JavaScript代码，在基准数据集上显著优于现有方法，证明了LLM去混淆和聚类级别关系建模的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着Web应用和云服务的快速发展，恶意JavaScript代码对用户隐私和系统安全构成严重威胁。然而，由于复杂的代码混淆技术、JavaScript固有的语言特性（如嵌套闭包结构、语法灵活性）以及抽象语法树（AST）中动态类型导致的语义分散和深层嵌套函数引起的作用域捕获中断，恶意代码检测仍然面临巨大挑战。

Method: 本文提出DeCoda混合防御框架，结合大型语言模型（LLM）的去混淆能力和代码图学习：1) 构建了一个多阶段细化提示学习流程，LLM逐步从混淆输入中重构原始代码结构，并生成标准化AST表示；2) 针对AST中存在的结构噪声和语义歧义，提出通过聚类图学习分层代码图表示，该方法协同集成图Transformer网络、节点聚类和节点到聚类注意力机制，以同时捕获本地节点级语义和全局聚类诱导的结构关系。

Conclusion: 实验结果凸显了基于LLM的去混淆的有效性，并强调了在恶意代码检测中建模聚类级别关系的重要性。

Abstract: With the rapid expansion of web-based applications and cloud services,
malicious JavaScript code continues to pose significant threats to user
privacy, system integrity, and enterprise security. But, detecting such threats
remains challenging due to sophisticated code obfuscation techniques and
JavaScript's inherent language characteristics, particularly its nested closure
structures and syntactic flexibility. In this work, we propose DeCoda, a hybrid
defense framework that combines large language model (LLM)-based deobfuscation
with code graph learning: (1) We first construct a sophisticated
prompt-learning pipeline with multi-stage refinement, where the LLM
progressively reconstructs the original code structure from obfuscated inputs
and then generates normalized Abstract Syntax Tree (AST) representations; (2)
In JavaScript ASTs, dynamic typing scatters semantically similar nodes while
deeply nested functions fracture scope capturing, introducing structural noise
and semantic ambiguity. To address these challenges, we then propose to learn
hierarchical code graph representations via a Cluster-wise Graph that
synergistically integrates graph transformer network, node clustering, and
node-to-cluster attention to simultaneously capture both local node-level
semantics and global cluster-induced structural relationships from AST graph.
Experimental results demonstrate that our method achieves F1-scores of 94.64%
and 97.71% on two benchmark datasets, demonstrating absolute improvements of
10.74% and 13.85% over state-of-the-art baselines. In false-positive control
evaluation at fixed FPR levels (0.0001, 0.001, 0.01), our approach delivers
4.82, 5.91, and 2.53 higher TPR respectively compared to the best-performing
baseline. These results highlight the effectiveness of LLM-based deobfuscation
and underscore the importance of modeling cluster-level relationships in
detecting malicious code.

### [240] [A surrogate model for topology optimisation of elastic structures via parametric autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22539)
*Matteo Giacomini,Antonio Huerta*

Conclusion: 所提出的基于代理模型的拓扑优化算法，通过结合学习预测和物理精修，有效加速了参数化线性弹性结构的拓扑优化过程，实现了计算效率的显著提升和高精度的保持，并展现出良好的泛化能力。

Abstract: A surrogate-based topology optimisation algorithm for linear elastic
structures under parametric loads and boundary conditions is proposed. Instead
of learning the parametric solution of the state (and adjoint) problems or the
optimisation trajectory as a function of the iterations, the proposed approach
devises a surrogate version of the entire optimisation pipeline. First, the
method predicts a quasi-optimal topology for a given problem configuration as a
surrogate model of high-fidelity topologies optimised with the homogenisation
method. This is achieved by means of a feed-forward net learning the mapping
between the input parameters characterising the system setup and a latent space
determined by encoder/decoder blocks reducing the dimensionality of the
parametric topology optimisation problem and reconstructing a high-dimensional
representation of the topology. Then, the predicted topology is used as an
educated initial guess for a computationally efficient algorithm penalising the
intermediate values of the design variable, while enforcing the governing
equations of the system. This step allows the method to correct potential
errors introduced by the surrogate model, eliminate artifacts, and refine the
design in order to produce topologies consistent with the underlying physics.

capabilities of the resulting models are numerically evaluated. The

reducing the average number of optimisation iterations by $53\%$ while
achieving discrepancies below $4\%$ in the optimal value of the objective
functional, even in the challenging scenario of testing the model to
extrapolate beyond the training and validation domain.

### [242] [Stacked SVD or SVD stacked? A Random Matrix Theory perspective on data integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22170)
*Tavor Z. Baharav,Phillip B. Nicol,Rafael A. Irizarry,Rong Ma*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文对两种常用的高维多数据集共享潜在结构识别方法（Stack-SVD和SVD-Stack）在比例渐近状态下的性能进行了理论分析和比较，并提出优化加权方案，发现优化加权Stack-SVD表现更优，为实际数据整合提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代数据分析常需识别高维多数据集中的共享潜在结构。Stack-SVD和SVD-Stack是两种主流方法，但其在比例渐近状态下的性能缺乏严格的理论研究，导致实际应用中选择困难，且限制了其潜力发挥。

Method: 研究者推导了Stack-SVD和SVD-Stack在渐近性能和相变方面的精确表达式，并开发了最优加权方案以改进两种方法。分析扩展至多共享分量情况，并提供了从数据中估计最优权重的实用算法。通过数值模拟和基因组半合成实验对理论发现进行了验证。

Result: 研究揭示，在未加权情况下，Stack-SVD和SVD-Stack均无绝对优势；然而，经最优加权后，Stack-SVD在性能上优于SVD-Stack。同时，研究还开发了适用于多共享分量的分析框架和实用的最优权重估计算法。

Conclusion: 本研究通过对Stack-SVD和SVD-Stack的严格理论分析和优化，尤其是在最优加权条件下，为解决实际数据整合问题中的方法选择提供了重要的理论指导，提升了这些方法的应用潜力。

Abstract: Modern data analysis increasingly requires identifying shared latent
structure across multiple high-dimensional datasets. A commonly used model
assumes that the data matrices are noisy observations of low-rank matrices with
a shared singular subspace. In this case, two primary methods have emerged for
estimating this shared structure, which vary in how they integrate information
across datasets. The first approach, termed Stack-SVD, concatenates all the
datasets, and then performs a singular value decomposition (SVD). The second
approach, termed SVD-Stack, first performs an SVD separately for each dataset,
then aggregates the top singular vectors across these datasets, and finally
computes a consensus amongst them. While these methods are widely used, they
have not been rigorously studied in the proportional asymptotic regime, which
is of great practical relevance in today's world of increasing data size and
dimensionality. This lack of theoretical understanding has led to uncertainty
about which method to choose and limited the ability to fully exploit their
potential. To address these challenges, we derive exact expressions for the
asymptotic performance and phase transitions of these two methods and develop
optimal weighting schemes to further improve both methods. Our analysis reveals
that while neither method uniformly dominates the other in the unweighted case,
optimally weighted Stack-SVD dominates optimally weighted SVD-Stack. We extend
our analysis to accommodate multiple shared components, and provide practical
algorithms for estimating optimal weights from data, offering theoretical
guidance for method selection in practical data integration problems. Extensive
numerical simulations and semi-synthetic experiments on genomic data
corroborate our theoretical findings.

</details>


### [243] [LVM-GP: Uncertainty-Aware PDE Solver via coupling latent variable model and Gaussian process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22493)
*Xiaodong Feng,Ling Guo,Xiaoliang Wan,Hao Wu,Tao Zhou,Wenwen Zhou*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 提出LVM-GP概率框架，结合潜在高斯过程和神经网络算子，以高效且鲁棒地量化含噪声偏微分方程（PDEs）求解的不确定性，并达到高预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在噪声数据下求解偏微分方程（PDEs）的正向和逆向问题时，有效量化不确定性（UQ）是一个重要挑战，现有方法可能无法充分捕获函数依赖性或提供鲁棒的UQ。

Method: 提出LVM-GP概率框架，核心是构建从输入到高维潜在表示的随机映射。架构包含：1. 置信度感知编码器：基于高斯过程的潜在变量模型，通过插值可学习确定性特征和高斯过程先验构建潜在表示，插值强度由学习到的置信函数自适应控制。2. 概率解码器：定义解场的条件高斯分布，均值由应用于潜在表示的神经网络算子预测。此外，物理定律作为软约束加入损失函数。

Result: 与贝叶斯物理信息神经网络（B-PINNs）和深度集成等现有方法相比，LVM-GP框架能有效捕获函数依赖关系，并实现具有竞争力的预测精度和鲁棒的不确定性量化。数值实验验证了其有效性和可靠性。

Conclusion: LVM-GP框架通过融合潜在高斯过程和神经网络算子，为解决含噪声数据的偏微分方程问题提供了一种高效、准确且可靠的不确定性量化方法。

Abstract: We propose a novel probabilistic framework, termed LVM-GP, for uncertainty
quantification in solving forward and inverse partial differential equations
(PDEs) with noisy data. The core idea is to construct a stochastic mapping from
the input to a high-dimensional latent representation, enabling
uncertainty-aware prediction of the solution. Specifically, the architecture
consists of a confidence-aware encoder and a probabilistic decoder. The encoder
implements a high-dimensional latent variable model based on a Gaussian process
(LVM-GP), where the latent representation is constructed by interpolating
between a learnable deterministic feature and a Gaussian process prior, with
the interpolation strength adaptively controlled by a confidence function
learned from data. The decoder defines a conditional Gaussian distribution over
the solution field, where the mean is predicted by a neural operator applied to
the latent representation, allowing the model to learn flexible
function-to-function mapping. Moreover, physical laws are enforced as soft
constraints in the loss function to ensure consistency with the underlying PDE
structure. Compared to existing approaches such as Bayesian physics-informed
neural networks (B-PINNs) and deep ensembles, the proposed framework can
efficiently capture functional dependencies via merging a latent Gaussian
process and neural operator, resulting in competitive predictive accuracy and
robust uncertainty quantification. Numerical experiments demonstrate the
effectiveness and reliability of the method.

</details>


### [244] [A Unified Analysis of Generalization and Sample Complexity for Semi-Supervised Domain Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22632)
*Elif Vural,Huseyin Karaca*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文对基于域对齐的域适应算法进行了全面的理论研究，推导了深度模型（MMD/对抗性）的泛化界限和样本复杂度，并提出了一种半监督设置下应对标记数据有限性的损失缩放策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 域适应领域的方法学发展迅速，但其理论基础相对未充分探索。现有理论多集中于简化场景，未能完全捕捉通过特征变换进行域对齐的现代方法的行为。

Method: 在半监督设置下，理论分析了域对齐特征变换与共享分类器的联合学习。首先，通过函数类的覆盖数推导了泛化界限；其次，通过对采用MMD或对抗性目标的域自适应神经网络架构的覆盖数进行严格分析，表征了其样本复杂度。

Result: 1) 基于MMD和对抗性模型的样本复杂度上限均与网络深度和宽度呈二次方关系。2) 在半监督设置下，通过将目标损失按标记目标样本数量的平方根比例缩放，可以实现对有限标记目标数据的鲁棒性。实验评估支持了这些理论发现。

Conclusion: 本文为基于域对齐的域适应算法提供了全面的理论框架，揭示了深度域适应模型的泛化和样本复杂度特性，并为半监督设置下的鲁棒性提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Domain adaptation seeks to leverage the abundant label information in a
source domain to improve classification performance in a target domain with
limited labels. While the field has seen extensive methodological development,
its theoretical foundations remain relatively underexplored. Most existing
theoretical analyses focus on simplified settings where the source and target
domains share the same input space and relate target-domain performance to
measures of domain discrepancy. Although insightful, these analyses may not
fully capture the behavior of modern approaches that align domains into a
shared space via feature transformations. In this paper, we present a
comprehensive theoretical study of domain adaptation algorithms based on domain
alignment. We consider the joint learning of domain-aligning feature
transformations and a shared classifier in a semi-supervised setting. We first
derive generalization bounds in a broad setting, in terms of covering numbers
of the relevant function classes. We then extend our analysis to characterize
the sample complexity of domain-adaptive neural networks employing maximum mean
discrepancy (MMD) or adversarial objectives. Our results rely on a rigorous
analysis of the covering numbers of these architectures. We show that, for both
MMD-based and adversarial models, the sample complexity admits an upper bound
that scales quadratically with network depth and width. Furthermore, our
analysis suggests that in semi-supervised settings, robustness to limited
labeled target data can be achieved by scaling the target loss proportionally
to the square root of the number of labeled target samples. Experimental
evaluation in both shallow and deep settings lends support to our theoretical
findings.

</details>

### [245] [Pathology Foundation Models are Scanner Sensitive: Benchmark and Mitigation with Contrastive ScanGen Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22092)
*Gianluca Carloni,Biagio Brattoli,Seongho Keum,Jongchan Park,Taebum Lee,Chang Ho Ahn,Sergio Pereira*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 针对计算病理学中的扫描仪偏差问题，本研究提出ScanGen对比损失函数，有效提高模型跨扫描仪的泛化能力，同时保持或提升预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习在计算病理学中虽表现出色，但易受扫描仪引入的无关细节影响，导致扫描仪偏差，进而降低临床医生对CPath工具的信任并阻碍其临床部署。即使是最新病理学基础模型也未能完全解决这一问题。

Method: 本研究首先使用多扫描仪数据集对病理学基础模型进行基准测试，确认其仍存在扫描仪偏差。在此基础上，提出ScanGen，一种在任务特定微调过程中应用的对比损失函数，旨在减轻扫描仪偏差，增强模型对扫描仪变异的鲁棒性。该方法应用于肺癌H&E染色全玻片图像的EGFR突变预测任务（多实例学习）。

Result: ScanGen显著增强了模型跨扫描仪的泛化能力，同时保持或改善了EGFR突变预测的性能。

Conclusion: ScanGen是一种有效减轻计算病理学模型扫描仪偏差的方法，能够显著提高模型的泛化能力和鲁棒性，从而有助于提升此类工具在临床实践中的可信度和部署潜力。

Abstract: Computational pathology (CPath) has shown great potential in mining
actionable insights from Whole Slide Images (WSIs). Deep Learning (DL) has been
at the center of modern CPath, and while it delivers unprecedented performance,
it is also known that DL may be affected by irrelevant details, such as those
introduced during scanning by different commercially available scanners. This
may lead to scanner bias, where the model outputs for the same tissue acquired
by different scanners may vary. In turn, it hinders the trust of clinicians in
CPath-based tools and their deployment in real-world clinical practices. Recent
pathology Foundation Models (FMs) promise to provide better domain
generalization capabilities. In this paper, we benchmark FMs using a
multi-scanner dataset and show that FMs still suffer from scanner bias.
Following this observation, we propose ScanGen, a contrastive loss function
applied during task-specific fine-tuning that mitigates scanner bias, thereby
enhancing the models' robustness to scanner variations. Our approach is applied
to the Multiple Instance Learning task of Epidermal Growth Factor Receptor
(EGFR) mutation prediction from H\&E-stained WSIs in lung cancer. We observe
that ScanGen notably enhances the ability to generalize across scanners, while
retaining or improving the performance of EGFR mutation prediction.

</details>

### [246] [aLLoyM: A large language model for alloy phase diagram prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22558)
*Yuna Oikawa,Guillaume Deffrennes,Taichi Abe,Ryo Tamura,Koji Tsuda*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: aLLoyM是一个基于合金组分、温度及相信息微调的大语言模型，显著提升了相图问题的回答准确性，并能生成新型相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLMs）在材料科学中具有广泛应用前景，本研究旨在开发一个专门针对合金相图信息的LLM，以加速新材料发现。

Method: 研究团队利用开源计算相图数据库（CPDDB）和CALPHAD评估结果，整理了二元和三元相图的问答对数据集。在此基础上，对开源预训练LLM Mistral进行了微调，训练了多项选择和简答两种格式的模型。

Result: 基准评估显示，微调显著提高了模型在多项选择相图问题上的性能。此外，aLLoyM的简答模型能够仅通过合金组分生成新颖的相图，展示了其在探索未知材料系统方面的潜力。

Conclusion: aLLoyM的开发证明了通过特定领域数据微调LLM在材料科学领域的巨大潜力，尤其是在加速新型材料系统发现方面。为推动研究和应用，模型及其完整基准数据集已公开。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are general-purpose tools with wide-ranging
applications, including in materials science. In this work, we introduce
aLLoyM, a fine-tuned LLM specifically trained on alloy compositions,
temperatures, and their corresponding phase information. To develop aLLoyM, we
curated question-and-answer (Q&A) pairs for binary and ternary phase diagrams
using the open-source Computational Phase Diagram Database (CPDDB) and
assessments based on CALPHAD (CALculation of PHAse Diagrams). We fine-tuned
Mistral, an open-source pre-trained LLM, for two distinct Q&A formats:
multiple-choice and short-answer. Benchmark evaluations demonstrate that
fine-tuning substantially enhances performance on multiple-choice phase diagram
questions. Moreover, the short-answer model of aLLoyM exhibits the ability to
generate novel phase diagrams from its components alone, underscoring its
potential to accelerate the discovery of previously unexplored materials
systems. To promote further research and adoption, we have publicly released
the short-answer fine-tuned version of aLLoyM, along with the complete
benchmarking Q&A dataset, on Hugging Face.

</details>

### [247] [Quantum-Inspired Audio Unlearning: Towards Privacy-Preserving Voice Biometrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22208)
*Shreyansh Pathak,Sonu Shreshtha,Richa Singh,Mayank Vatsa*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出QPAudioEraser，一个量子启发的音频遗忘框架，旨在高效彻底地从语音生物识别模型中擦除特定个体数据，以满足隐私法规要求，同时最小化对模型性能的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语音认证和生物识别系统普及，敏感语音数据面临严重的隐私漏洞。GDPR等隐私法规要求从已训练模型中高效擦除特定个体语音签名。然而，现有遗忘方法不足以处理音频数据的序列性、时序性和高维特性，导致无法有效或完整地擦除说话人及口音信息。

Method: 本研究引入QPAudioEraser，一个量子启发的音频遗忘框架。其四阶段方法包括：1) 使用相消干涉进行权重初始化以抵消目标特征；2) 基于叠加的标签转换以模糊类别身份；3) 应用不确定性最大化的量子损失函数；4) 受纠缠启发的加权混合以保留模型知识。

Result: 通过在ResNet18、ViT和CNN架构上，以及AudioMNIST、Speech Commands、LibriSpeech和Speech Accent Archive数据集上的综合评估，QPAudioEraser实现了目标数据的完全擦除（0%遗忘准确率），同时对模型效用影响极小，保留数据性能下降低至0.05%。在单类别、多类别、序列和口音级别擦除场景中，QPAudioEraser始终优于传统基线。

Conclusion: QPAudioEraser被确立为一个强大的隐私保护解决方案，能够有效解决音频生物识别系统中的数据遗忘问题，并满足相关隐私法规要求。

Abstract: The widespread adoption of voice-enabled authentication and audio biometric
systems have significantly increased privacy vulnerabilities associated with
sensitive speech data. Compliance with privacy regulations such as GDPR's right
to be forgotten and India's DPDP Act necessitates targeted and efficient
erasure of individual-specific voice signatures from already-trained biometric
models. Existing unlearning methods designed for visual data inadequately
handle the sequential, temporal, and high-dimensional nature of audio signals,
leading to ineffective or incomplete speaker and accent erasure. To address
this, we introduce QPAudioEraser, a quantum-inspired audio unlearning
framework. Our our-phase approach involves: (1) weight initialization using
destructive interference to nullify target features, (2) superposition-based
label transformations that obscure class identity, (3) an
uncertainty-maximizing quantum loss function, and (4) entanglement-inspired
mixing of correlated weights to retain model knowledge. Comprehensive
evaluations with ResNet18, ViT, and CNN architectures across AudioMNIST, Speech
Commands, LibriSpeech, and Speech Accent Archive datasets validate
QPAudioEraser's superior performance. The framework achieves complete erasure
of target data (0% Forget Accuracy) while incurring minimal impact on model
utility, with a performance degradation on retained data as low as 0.05%.
QPAudioEraser consistently surpasses conventional baselines across
single-class, multi-class, sequential, and accent-level erasure scenarios,
establishing the proposed approach as a robust privacy-preserving solution.

</details>


### [248] [Next Tokens Denoising for Speech Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.22746)
*Yanqing Liu,Ruiqing Xue,Chong Zhang,Yufei Liu,Gang Wang,Bohan Li,Yao Qian,Lei He,Shujie Liu,Sheng Zhao*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: Dragon-FM模型创新性地结合自回归与流匹配，实现了高效、高质量的文本到语音转换，尤其擅长生成长篇内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归（AR）模型生成速度慢且无法利用未来上下文，而扩散模型在键值（KV）缓存方面存在困难，现有生成模型存在明显局限。

Method: 提出Dragon-FM，一种新型文本到语音（TTS）设计，将自回归（AR）与流匹配（flow-matching）模型相结合。该模型以块（chunks）处理48 kHz音频编解码器token，通过跨块的AR建模确保全局连贯性，同时利用块内并行流匹配实现快速迭代去噪。

Result: Dragon-FM能够跨块利用KV缓存，并在块内融入未来上下文。它还弥合了连续与离散特征建模的鸿沟，能够用连续AR流匹配预测离散token。该模型特别适用于生成扩展内容，在播客数据集上的实验表明其能高效生成高质量的零样本播客。

Conclusion: Dragon-FM通过结合自回归和流匹配的优势，有效克服了现有生成模型的局限性，为高效、高质量的文本到语音转换（特别是长内容）提供了一种强大且创新的解决方案。

Abstract: While diffusion and autoregressive (AR) models have significantly advanced
generative modeling, they each present distinct limitations. AR models, which
rely on causal attention, cannot exploit future context and suffer from slow
generation speeds. Conversely, diffusion models struggle with key-value (KV)
caching. To overcome these challenges, we introduce Dragon-FM, a novel
text-to-speech (TTS) design that unifies AR and flow-matching. This model
processes 48 kHz audio codec tokens in chunks at a compact 12.5 tokens per
second rate. This design enables AR modeling across chunks, ensuring global
coherence, while parallel flow-matching within chunks facilitates fast
iterative denoising. Consequently, the proposed model can utilize KV-cache
across chunks and incorporate future context within each chunk. Furthermore, it
bridges continuous and discrete feature modeling, demonstrating that continuous
AR flow-matching can predict discrete tokens with finite scalar quantizers.
This efficient codec and fast chunk-autoregressive architecture also makes the
proposed model particularly effective for generating extended content.
Experiment for demos of our work} on podcast datasets demonstrate its
capability to efficiently generate high-quality zero-shot podcasts.

</details>
